## Feasibility Assessment: Online Apparels Shopping Website

Based on the provided Functional Specification Document (FSD), here's a feasibility assessment for the proposed Online Apparels Shopping Website:

**1. Technical Feasibility:**

The project appears technically feasible. The requirements outlined in the FSD are common in e-commerce development and can be achieved using standard technologies and practices. There are no immediately apparent technical blockers. The integration with Stripe is a well-documented and established process.

**2. Key Risks:**

- **Integration Complexity**: Integrating with third-party services like Stripe, Facebook, and Google for authentication and payment processing can introduce unexpected complexities and dependencies. Thorough testing and robust error handling are crucial.
- **Scalability**: The document doesn't address scalability concerns. As the user base and product catalog grow, the system's performance might degrade if not designed with scalability in mind. Database optimization, caching strategies, and load balancing may be required.
- **Security**: E-commerce platforms handle sensitive user data (personal information, payment details). Security vulnerabilities can lead to data breaches and reputational damage. Implementing robust security measures (e.g., encryption, secure coding practices, regular security audits) is essential.
- **Performance**: Slow loading times and poor performance can negatively impact user experience and conversion rates. Optimizing the frontend and backend for speed and efficiency is crucial.
- **Third-Party API Changes**: Reliance on external APIs (Stripe, Facebook, Google) means the application is vulnerable to changes in these APIs, potentially requiring code modifications and updates.

**3. Budget & Resource Needs:**

- **Frontend Developers**: 2-3 developers with expertise in HTML, CSS, JavaScript, and a modern JavaScript framework (e.g., React, Angular, Vue.js).
- **Backend Developers**: 2-3 developers proficient in a backend language (e.g., Python, Java, Node.js), a database (e.g., MySQL, PostgreSQL, MongoDB), and RESTful API development.
- **QA Testers**: 1-2 testers to ensure the quality and functionality of the application.
- **UI/UX Designer**: 1 designer to create a user-friendly and visually appealing interface.
- **Project Manager**: 1 project manager to oversee the project and ensure it stays on track.
- **DevOps Engineer**: 1 DevOps engineer to handle deployment, infrastructure, and system maintenance.
- **Infrastructure Costs**: Hosting, domain registration, SSL certificate, CDN (Content Delivery Network).
- **Third-Party Service Fees**: Stripe transaction fees, API usage costs.
- **Contingency**: A buffer for unexpected issues and changes.

Based on the scope and complexity, a rough estimate for the development cost would be between **$50,000 and $150,000**, depending on the team's location, experience, and the chosen technologies.

**4. Recommended Timeline:**

- **Phase 1 (Planning & Design)**: 2-4 weeks (Requirements refinement, UI/UX design, database design, technology selection).
- **Phase 2 (Frontend Development)**: 6-10 weeks (Implement the user interface, integrate with backend APIs).
- **Phase 3 (Backend Development)**: 6-10 weeks (Develop the backend logic, database interactions, API endpoints).
- **Phase 4 (Integration & Testing)**: 4-6 weeks (Integrate frontend and backend, conduct thorough testing, fix bugs).
- **Phase 5 (Deployment & Launch)**: 2-4 weeks (Deploy the application to production, monitor performance, address any issues).

**Total Estimated Timeline: 4-6 months**. This is a high-level estimate and could vary based on the project's specific requirements and the team's efficiency.

**5. Critical Questions:**

1.  **Technology Stack**: What specific technologies (programming languages, frameworks, databases, cloud platforms) will be used for the frontend and backend development? A detailed technology stack needs to be defined.
    - Answer: Frontend: Next.js (React, TypeScript) + Tailwind; Backend: NestJS (Node, TypeScript) with REST + webhooks; DB: PostgreSQL (AWS RDS) via Prisma; Cache: Redis (ElastiCache); Search: Algolia/OpenSearch; Storage: S3; Auth: NextAuth/Auth0; Hosting: Vercel (FE) + AWS ECS Fargate or Lambda (BE); CI/CD: GitHub Actions; IaC: Terraform.
2.  **Scalability Strategy**: What measures will be taken to ensure the system can handle increasing traffic and data volume? What is the expected growth rate?
    - Answer: CDN + ISR for pages, stateless autoscaled services, Redis caching, DB indexing/read replicas/pooling, SQS-based async processing with idempotency, search offloaded to Algolia/OpenSearch; revisit capacity quarterly.
3.  **Security Measures**: What security protocols and practices will be implemented to protect user data and prevent vulnerabilities? What compliance standards need to be met?
    - Answer: Enforce HTTPS/TLS, CSP/HSTS headers, CSRF protection, RBAC + MFA for admin, input validation, encryption at rest (KMS) and in transit, secrets in AWS Secrets Manager, SAST/DAST + dependency scanning, centralized logging/monitoring; Compliance: PCI-DSS SAQ A, GDPR (SOC 2 if required).
4.  **Deployment Environment**: Where will the application be hosted (e.g., AWS, Azure, Google Cloud)? What is the deployment process?
    - Answer: AWS + Vercel: Vercel for frontend; AWS (ECS Fargate/Lambda, RDS, ElastiCache, S3, CloudFront, WAF) for backend/data; CI/CD via GitHub Actions + Terraform, environments (dev/stage/prod), blue/green or canary with automated rollback.
5.  **Maintenance and Support**: What are the plans for ongoing maintenance, bug fixes, and feature updates after the initial launch? Is there a dedicated support team?
    - Answer: On-call rotation with runbooks, defined SLOs/error budgets, weekly dependency/security updates, automated backups + DR drills, analytics-driven roadmap; Support tiers T1/T2/T3 with SLAs.
6.  **Payment Gateway Configuration**: What are the specific requirements and configurations for the Stripe payment gateway integration? What fraud prevention measures will be in place?
    - Answer: Stripe Payment Intents via Checkout (or Elements), SCA/3DS, idempotency keys, signed webhooks (checkout.session.completed, payment_intent.\*), Radar rules + AVS/CVV, multi-currency and Stripe Tax as needed, admin refunds/disputes.
7.  **Shipping Integration**: How will shipping be handled? Will there be integration with any shipping providers for automated shipping label generation and tracking?
    - Answer: Use a shipping aggregator (EasyPost/Shippo) for real-time rates, label purchase, tracking webhooks, returns; address validation, packaging presets, and international customs/duties support as needed.  - Identify dependencies and constraints

  - Propose milestones with specific deliverables and responsible parties

---  - Create a phased timeline with deadlines

  - Identify scope (must-have, nice-to-have, not-in-scope)

**Title:** Functional Specification Document: Online Apparels Shopping Website

**Summary:** This document details the functional specifications for the development of an Online Apparels Shopping Website, an e-commerce platform. It outlines the features for both the frontend website for buyers and the web-based backend/admin panel for the business owner.


### Non-Functional Requirement Document.pdf (requirements_document)

**Title:** Non-Functional Requirement Document: Online Apparels Shopping Website

**Summary:** This document specifies the non-functional requirements (NFRs) for the Online Apparels Shopping Website. These requirements define criteria used to judge the system's operation rather than specific behaviors, focusing on aspects like performance, security, scalability, and usability.


### online_apparels_shopping_website.pdf (business_requirements)

**Title:** Online Apparels shopping Website Business Requirements Document

**Summary:** This document outlines the business requirements for an online ecommerce website for selling apparels. It details the objectives, scope, user roles, and functional and non-functional requirements for both buyers and administrators.


### Technical Specification Document.pdf (technical_specification)

**Title:** Technical Specification Document: Online Apparels Shopping Website

**Summary:** This document outlines the technical specifications for an online apparel shopping website. It details the system architecture, technology stack, data model, frontend and backend specifications, as well as constraints and risks.


### Test Plan.pdf (test_plan)

**Title:** Test Plan / QA Documentation: Online Apparels Shopping Website

**Summary:** This Test Plan outlines the strategy, scope, resources, and schedule for testing the Online Apparels Shopping Website. The primary goal is to verify that the developed system meets all specified Functional Requirements (FRs), adheres to Non-Functional Requirements (NFRs), and satisfies the overall Business Requirements Document (BRD) objectives.


### Use Case.pdf (use_case)

**Title:** Online Apparels Shopping Website Use Cases

**Summary:** This document outlines the use cases for an online apparels shopping website. It details the interactions of different actors, including Guest Users, Buyers, and Admin, with the system, covering functionalities like product discovery, registration, purchasing, order fulfillment, and system maintenance.


## Requirements

1. [CRITICAL / functional] Login: Users shall be able to log in using their registered email and password. A 'Reset Password' option shall be available. Users must also be able to log in using Facebook and Google accounts.
2. [CRITICAL / functional] Registration: Buyers must register using a simple form (First name, Last name, Email ID, Contact number, Password, Conform password). They must accept terms and conditions. Email ID verification is mandatory before the user can log in.
3. [CRITICAL / functional] My Account: Logged-in buyers can access and manage their Profile details (email, phone number), change password, view/manage Addresses, My Orders, My Wishlist, Shopping Cart, and Ratings and reviews.
4. [CRITICAL / functional] Product Search: Buyers/Guests can search for products by keyword, browsing category/sub-category, and using filters and sorting options. Searching is available without login.
5. [CRITICAL / functional] Product Listing: The product listing page shall display the Product title, Thumbnail image, Price, and Ratings & reviews.
6. [CRITICAL / functional] Product Details: The product details page shall display Product title, Thumbnail image, Product images, Product description, Price, available Sizes/colors (variations), and Ratings & reviews. Users can check shipping availability by entering a PIN code.
7. [HIGH / functional] Wishlist: Buyers can view, add, or delete products from their wishlist. Products in the wishlist can be moved to the shopping cart for checkout. Adding to wishlist is not possible without login.
8. [CRITICAL / functional] Shopping Cart: Users can add/remove items and update the quantity of items. The cart shall display the item price, sub-total, and total price.
9. [CRITICAL / functional] Checkout & Payment: Before payment, the buyer must enter billing and shipping addresses. Payment methods must include Credit card/debit card and Net banking. The order summary shall display Item total, Sub-total, Shipping cost, Tax, and Order total. Stripe payment gateway will be integrated for online payment.
10. [CRITICAL / functional] Order History & Tracking: Buyers can view a list of all past orders and detailed information. Users can track the status of their current orders and reorder items from past order details. Order status updates will trigger email notifications.
11. [HIGH / functional] Ratings & Reviews: Users can only post ratings and reviews for products they have previously ordered from the website.
12. [LOW / functional] Social Media Sharing: Buyers/Guests can share products on social media. Login is not mandatory.
13. [HIGH / functional] Contact Support: Buyers/Guests can contact support via email for queries/complaints by submitting their name, email, contact number, and message. Admin will receive an email with the complaint details.
14. [CRITICAL / functional] Admin Login: Admin/Sub-users can log in using a username and password. A 'Reset Password' option shall be available.
15. [CRITICAL / functional] Dashboard: The Admin Dashboard shall display key metrics: Total no. of active and inactive registered buyers, Total no. of Products uploaded, and Total Revenue (today/this month).
16. [CRITICAL / functional] Products Management: Admin can Add/Edit/Active/Inactive products in the catalog. Information managed includes Product name, Images, Description, Keywords, and Variations (color, size).
17. [CRITICAL / functional] Product Categories Management: Admin can Add/Edit/Active/Inactive product categories and sub-categories.
18. [CRITICAL / functional] Orders Management: Admin can view a list of all orders with their current status, view/edit order details, and update the order status. Possible statuses are: Open, Confirmed, In process, Shipped, and Delivered.
19. [CRITICAL / functional] Shipping Management: Admin is responsible for order shipment and shall maintain shipment details: Shipping carrier, Tracking ID, Current status of shipment, Delivery location/address, and Shipping cost.
20. [CRITICAL / functional] Buyers Management: Admin can view/edit/activate/inactivate buyer account information, including profile details, address, orders, wishlist, and items in cart.
21. [MEDIUM / functional] Ratings & Review Management: Admin can approve/reject ratings and reviews posted by the buyers for products.
22. [CRITICAL / functional] Payment Management: Admin can view/edit bank account details (to receive payments) and view the payment status of each order. Stripe payment gateway will be used.
23. [CRITICAL / functional] CMS Management: Admin can edit the content for the following CMS pages: About us, Contact us, Privacy policy, and Terms and conditions.
24. [HIGH / functional] Statistics & Reports: Admin can view reports on Products uploaded (filterable by Date: From-To, Month, Year) and Revenue/total sale (filterable by Today, Current week, Date: From-To, Month, Year). Reports can be exported to PDF and Excel formats.
25. [HIGH / functional] System Users Management: Admin can create/edit/delete/activate/inactivate sub-users for various sectional operations.
26. [HIGH / functional] Roles Management: Admin can add/edit/delete/activate/inactivate sub-admin users with role-based access.
27. [HIGH / functional] Complaints/Feedbacks: Admin can view queries/complaints/feedbacks received from buyers (via FR-013). The admin will also receive an email notification for each submission.
28. [MEDIUM / functional] Email Management: Admin can add/edit/delete content for emails to be sent to buyers regarding new product launch, offers, and promotions.
29. [MEDIUM / non-functional] Scalability: The website repository shall accommodate up to 100 concurrent users.
30. [MEDIUM / non-functional] Speed/Performance: Web pages should load in less than 3 seconds under good internet speed.
31. [MEDIUM / non-functional] Reliability/Availability: Web pages must not display "page not found" errors for non-existent pages.
32. [MEDIUM / non-functional] Security: SSL security and encryption are mandatory for online payments.
33. [HIGH / non-functional] Page Load Speed shall not exceed 3 seconds.
34. [HIGH / non-functional] API Response Time shall not exceed 500 milliseconds.
35. [HIGH / non-functional] Search Latency shall not exceed 1 second.
36. [HIGH / non-functional] Must accommodate up to 100 users concurrently.
37. [HIGH / non-functional] Must support a minimum of 150 orders per hour.
38. [HIGH / non-functional] Must support a minimum of 10,000 product SKUs.
39. [HIGH / non-functional] SSL security and encryption (Minimum TLS 1.2).
40. [HIGH / non-functional] Passwords must be stored using a one-way hashing algorithm (e.g., bcrypt or Argon2) with salt.
41. [HIGH / non-functional] Must enforce Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) for all Admin and Sub-user functions.
42. [HIGH / non-functional] System must enforce input validation against SQL Injection and Cross-Site Scripting (XSS) on all user and admin inputs.
43. [HIGH / non-functional] 99.9% uptime during core business hours (9 AM - 5 PM EST).
44. [HIGH / non-functional] Web pages should not get broken and must display an appropriate "Page Not Found" error.
45. [HIGH / non-functional] Daily full backup; retention for 30 days.
46. [HIGH / non-functional] Must log all create/edit/delete operations performed by Admin and Sub-users.
47. [HIGH / non-functional] All configurable values (e.g., Tax rates, Shipping carrier details, Email content) must be managed via the Admin Panel.
48. [HIGH / non-functional] Codebase must adhere to [Specific Language] coding standards (e.g., PEP8 for Python) and pass peer review.
49. [HIGH / non-functional] US country only. System must validate shipping addresses for US residency.
50. [HIGH / non-functional] All product prices will be in USD.
51. [HIGH / non-functional] CMS pages for Privacy Policy and Terms and Conditions must be accessible and editable by the Admin.
52. [1 / functional] User will be able to login into the website using the email and password. Reset password option for the users to reset the password in case of forgot password. User will also be able to login into website using Facebook and Google account.
53. [1 / functional] Buyers will be able to get registered on website with simple registration form. Email id verification would be mandatory to get login into website.
54. [1 / functional] Buyers will be able to search the products by keyword, by browsing through category/sub-category, using filters and sorting options. User would be able to search for the products without login into website.
55. [1 / functional] Buyers will be able to view the listing of the product with details like product title, thumbnail image, price, ratings & reviews. User should be able to view the products listing and details without login.
56. [1 / functional] User would be able to view all product details on this page. Login will not be required to view the product details. User will be able to check the shipping availability by entering PIN code. User will be able to add the product to his shopping cart and wishlist. User will be able to share product on social media.
57. [2 / functional] Buyer will need to get registered and login into website to maintain his list of items in wishlist. Buyer will be able to view/ add/delete products added into his wishlist. User will be able to proceed for checkout process of items available in wishlist.
58. [1 / functional] The products can be added into shopping cart from the product detail page. User is required to get register and login to manage the items in his shopping cart. User will be able to add items/remove items/ update quantity of items in shopping cart. User will be able to proceed for checkout of any items/ all items available in shopping cart.

## Features

1. **Account Management (Login/Registration)**: Allows users to log in, register, and manage their account details.
2. **Product Search**: Enables buyers/guests to search for products by keyword, category, and filters.
3. **Product Listing**: Displays product information such as title, image, price, and ratings.
4. **Product Details**: Shows detailed information about a product, including images, description, price, and variations.
5. **Wishlist**: Allows buyers to add products to their wishlist.
6. **Shopping Cart**: Enables users to add/remove items and update quantities in their shopping cart.
7. **Checkout & Payment**: Facilitates the checkout process, including billing/shipping address input and online payment.
8. **Order History & Tracking**: Allows buyers to view their past orders and track the status of current orders.
9. **Ratings & Reviews**: Enables users to post ratings and reviews for products.

49. **Roles Management**: Allows the admin to manage roles and permissions for sub-users.
50. **CMS Management**: Allows the admin to edit content for CMS pages like About Us and Contact Us.
51. **Email Management**: Allows the admin to manage email content for promotions and notifications.
52. **Complaints/Feedbacks**: Allows the admin to view and respond to buyer complaints and feedback.
53. **Search Functionality**: Implement a server-side full-text search engine to handle keyword and category search efficiently.
54. **Product Variations**: The Product Details Page must dynamically handle color and size variations and update the display based on availability.
55. **Shipping Check**: An API call must be made to a shipping service or internal table based on the entered PIN code to check availability.
56. **Login/Registration**: Implement OAuth 2.0 or OpenID Connect flows for third-party logins. Passwords must be hashed and salted.
57. **Mandatory Verification**: Implement an asynchronous job or service to send the email verification link upon registration.
58. **Secure Transactions**: All checkout and payment pages must enforce HTTPS and interact with the Stripe API securely using tokens.
59. **Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)**: Implement a granular RBAC system allowing the main Admin to create sub-users and assign them specific roles/permissions.
60. **Catalog Management**: Utilize a Content Management System (CMS) interface within the Admin Panel to manage product attributes.
61. **Inventory Integration**: The system will use the Product Code (SKU) as the key for integrating with any future inventory management tools.
62. **Order Status Workflow**: Implement a state machine for order status transitions with automated email notifications to the buyer upon each change.
63. **Data Aggregation**: Implement a data layer optimized for reporting to quickly generate reports for Products Uploaded and Revenue/Total Sale.
64. **Export Functionality**: Use a library to generate and export reports into standard PDF and Excel formats.
65. **Registration**: User registration functionality.
66. **Login (Email/Social)**: User login functionality using email or social media accounts.
67. **Product Search/Listing**: Functionality to search and list products.
68. **Product Details/Variations**: Displaying product details and variations.
69. **Shopping Cart**: Functionality to add and manage items in a shopping cart.
70. **Wishlist**: Functionality to save products to a wishlist.
71. **Checkout**: Checkout process for ordering products.
72. **Online Payment (Stripe)**: Online payment processing using Stripe.
73. **Order Tracking**: Functionality to track orders.
74. **Ratings & Reviews**: Functionality to rate and review products.
75. **My Account/Address Book**: User account management and address book.
76. **Admin Login**: Admin login functionality.
77. **Dashboard**: Admin dashboard with key metrics.
78. **Product/Category Management**: Functionality to manage products and categories.
79. **Orders Management**: Functionality to manage orders.
80. **Customer Management**: Functionality to manage customers.
81. **Shipping/Payment Management**: Functionality to manage shipping and payment options.
82. **CMS**: Content Management System for managing website content.
83. **Roles/Permissions**: Functionality to manage user roles and permissions.
84. **Reporting (Statistics)**: Reporting and statistics functionality.

## Feasibility Assessment: Online Apparels Shopping Website

Based on the provided Functional Specification Document (FSD), here's a feasibility assessment for the proposed Online Apparels Shopping Website:

**1. Technical Feasibility:**

The project appears technically feasible. The requirements outlined in the FSD are common in e-commerce development and can be achieved using standard technologies and practices. There are no immediately apparent technical blockers. The integration with Stripe is a well-documented and established process.

**2. Key Risks:**

- **Integration Complexity**: Integrating with third-party services like Stripe, Facebook, and Google for authentication and payment processing can introduce unexpected complexities and dependencies. Thorough testing and robust error handling are crucial.
- **Scalability**: The document doesn't address scalability concerns. As the user base and product catalog grow, the system's performance might degrade if not designed with scalability in mind. Database optimization, caching strategies, and load balancing may be required.
- **Security**: E-commerce platforms handle sensitive user data (personal information, payment details). Security vulnerabilities can lead to data breaches and reputational damage. Implementing robust security measures (e.g., encryption, secure coding practices, regular security audits) is essential.
- **Performance**: Slow loading times and poor performance can negatively impact user experience and conversion rates. Optimizing the frontend and backend for speed and efficiency is crucial.
- **Third-Party API Changes**: Reliance on external APIs (Stripe, Facebook, Google) means the application is vulnerable to changes in these APIs, potentially requiring code modifications and updates.

**3. Budget & Resource Needs:**

- **Frontend Developers**: 2-3 developers with expertise in HTML, CSS, JavaScript, and a modern JavaScript framework (e.g., React, Angular, Vue.js).
- **Backend Developers**: 2-3 developers proficient in a backend language (e.g., Python, Java, Node.js), a database (e.g., MySQL, PostgreSQL, MongoDB), and RESTful API development.
- **QA Testers**: 1-2 testers to ensure the quality and functionality of the application.
- **UI/UX Designer**: 1 designer to create a user-friendly and visually appealing interface.
- **Project Manager**: 1 project manager to oversee the project and ensure it stays on track.
- **DevOps Engineer**: 1 DevOps engineer to handle deployment, infrastructure, and system maintenance.
- **Infrastructure Costs**: Hosting, domain registration, SSL certificate, CDN (Content Delivery Network).
- **Third-Party Service Fees**: Stripe transaction fees, API usage costs.
- **Contingency**: A buffer for unexpected issues and changes.

Based on the scope and complexity, a rough estimate for the development cost would be between **$50,000 and $150,000**, depending on the team's location, experience, and the chosen technologies.

**4. Recommended Timeline:**

- **Phase 1 (Planning & Design)**: 2-4 weeks (Requirements refinement, UI/UX design, database design, technology selection).
- **Phase 2 (Frontend Development)**: 6-10 weeks (Implement the user interface, integrate with backend APIs).
- **Phase 3 (Backend Development)**: 6-10 weeks (Develop the backend logic, database interactions, API endpoints).
- **Phase 4 (Integration & Testing)**: 4-6 weeks (Integrate frontend and backend, conduct thorough testing, fix bugs).
- **Phase 5 (Deployment & Launch)**: 2-4 weeks (Deploy the application to production, monitor performance, address any issues).

**Total Estimated Timeline: 4-6 months**. This is a high-level estimate and could vary based on the project's specific requirements and the team's efficiency.

**5. Critical Questions:**

1.  **Technology Stack**: What specific technologies (programming languages, frameworks, databases, cloud platforms) will be used for the frontend and backend development? A detailed technology stack needs to be defined.
    - Answer: Frontend: Next.js (React, TypeScript) + Tailwind; Backend: NestJS (Node, TypeScript) with REST + webhooks; DB: PostgreSQL (AWS RDS) via Prisma; Cache: Redis (ElastiCache); Search: Algolia/OpenSearch; Storage: S3; Auth: NextAuth/Auth0; Hosting: Vercel (FE) + AWS ECS Fargate or Lambda (BE); CI/CD: GitHub Actions; IaC: Terraform.
2.  **Scalability Strategy**: What measures will be taken to ensure the system can handle increasing traffic and data volume? What is the expected growth rate?
    - Answer: CDN + ISR for pages, stateless autoscaled services, Redis caching, DB indexing/read replicas/pooling, SQS-based async processing with idempotency, search offloaded to Algolia/OpenSearch; revisit capacity quarterly.
3.  **Security Measures**: What security protocols and practices will be implemented to protect user data and prevent vulnerabilities? What compliance standards need to be met?
    - Answer: Enforce HTTPS/TLS, CSP/HSTS headers, CSRF protection, RBAC + MFA for admin, input validation, encryption at rest (KMS) and in transit, secrets in AWS Secrets Manager, SAST/DAST + dependency scanning, centralized logging/monitoring; Compliance: PCI-DSS SAQ A, GDPR (SOC 2 if required).
4.  **Deployment Environment**: Where will the application be hosted (e.g., AWS, Azure, Google Cloud)? What is the deployment process?
    - Answer: AWS + Vercel: Vercel for frontend; AWS (ECS Fargate/Lambda, RDS, ElastiCache, S3, CloudFront, WAF) for backend/data; CI/CD via GitHub Actions + Terraform, environments (dev/stage/prod), blue/green or canary with automated rollback.
5.  **Maintenance and Support**: What are the plans for ongoing maintenance, bug fixes, and feature updates after the initial launch? Is there a dedicated support team?
    - Answer: On-call rotation with runbooks, defined SLOs/error budgets, weekly dependency/security updates, automated backups + DR drills, analytics-driven roadmap; Support tiers T1/T2/T3 with SLAs.
6.  **Payment Gateway Configuration**: What are the specific requirements and configurations for the Stripe payment gateway integration? What fraud prevention measures will be in place?
    - Answer: Stripe Payment Intents via Checkout (or Elements), SCA/3DS, idempotency keys, signed webhooks (checkout.session.completed, payment_intent.\*), Radar rules + AVS/CVV, multi-currency and Stripe Tax as needed, admin refunds/disputes.
7.  **Shipping Integration**: How will shipping be handled? Will there be integration with any shipping providers for automated shipping label generation and tracking?
    - Answer: Use a shipping aggregator (EasyPost/Shippo) for real-time rates, label purchase, tracking webhooks, returns; address validation, packaging presets, and international customs/duties support as needed.

Do not enclose the final content in backticks.

### Use Case.pdf (use_case)

**Title:** Online Apparels Shopping Website Use Cases

**Summary:** This document outlines the use cases for an online apparels shopping website. It details the interactions of different actors, including Guest Users, Buyers, and Admin, with the system, covering functionalities like product discovery, registration, purchasing, order fulfillment, and system maintenance.


## Requirements

1. [CRITICAL / functional] Login: Users shall be able to log in using their registered email and password. A 'Reset Password' option shall be available. Users must also be able to log in using Facebook and Google accounts.
2. [CRITICAL / functional] Registration: Buyers must register using a simple form (First name, Last name, Email ID, Contact number, Password, Conform password). They must accept terms and conditions. Email ID verification is mandatory before the user can log in.
3. [CRITICAL / functional] My Account: Logged-in buyers can access and manage their Profile details (email, phone number), change password, view/manage Addresses, My Orders, My Wishlist, Shopping Cart, and Ratings and reviews.
4. [CRITICAL / functional] Product Search: Buyers/Guests can search for products by keyword, browsing category/sub-category, and using filters and sorting options. Searching is available without login.
5. [CRITICAL / functional] Product Listing: The product listing page shall display the Product title, Thumbnail image, Price, and Ratings & reviews.
6. [CRITICAL / functional] Product Details: The product details page shall display Product title, Thumbnail image, Product images, Product description, Price, available Sizes/colors (variations), and Ratings & reviews. Users can check shipping availability by entering a PIN code.
7. [HIGH / functional] Wishlist: Buyers can view, add, or delete products from their wishlist. Products in the wishlist can be moved to the shopping cart for checkout. Adding to wishlist is not possible without login.
8. [CRITICAL / functional] Shopping Cart: Users can add/remove items and update the quantity of items. The cart shall display the item price, sub-total, and total price.
9. [CRITICAL / functional] Checkout & Payment: Before payment, the buyer must enter billing and shipping addresses. Payment methods must include Credit card/debit card and Net banking. The order summary shall display Item total, Sub-total, Shipping cost, Tax, and Order total. Stripe payment gateway will be integrated for online payment.
10. [CRITICAL / functional] Order History & Tracking: Buyers can view a list of all past orders and detailed information. Users can track the status of their current orders and reorder items from past order details. Order status updates will trigger email notifications.
11. [HIGH / functional] Ratings & Reviews: Users can only post ratings and reviews for products they have previously ordered from the website.
12. [LOW / functional] Social Media Sharing: Buyers/Guests can share products on social media. Login is not mandatory.
13. [HIGH / functional] Contact Support: Buyers/Guests can contact support via email for queries/complaints by submitting their name, email, contact number, and message. Admin will receive an email with the complaint details.
14. [CRITICAL / functional] Admin Login: Admin/Sub-users can log in using a username and password. A 'Reset Password' option shall be available.
15. [CRITICAL / functional] Dashboard: The Admin Dashboard shall display key metrics: Total no. of active and inactive registered buyers, Total no. of Products uploaded, and Total Revenue (today/this month).
16. [CRITICAL / functional] Products Management: Admin can Add/Edit/Active/Inactive products in the catalog. Information managed includes Product name, Images, Description, Keywords, and Variations (color, size).
17. [CRITICAL / functional] Product Categories Management: Admin can Add/Edit/Active/Inactive product categories and sub-categories.
18. [CRITICAL / functional] Orders Management: Admin can view a list of all orders with their current status, view/edit order details, and update the order status. Possible statuses are: Open, Confirmed, In process, Shipped, and Delivered.
19. [CRITICAL / functional] Shipping Management: Admin is responsible for order shipment and shall maintain shipment details: Shipping carrier, Tracking ID, Current status of shipment, Delivery location/address, and Shipping cost.
20. [CRITICAL / functional] Buyers Management: Admin can view/edit/activate/inactivate buyer account information, including profile details, address, orders, wishlist, and items in cart.
21. [MEDIUM / functional] Ratings & Review Management: Admin can approve/reject ratings and reviews posted by the buyers for products.
22. [CRITICAL / functional] Payment Management: Admin can view/edit bank account details (to receive payments) and view the payment status of each order. Stripe payment gateway will be used.
23. [CRITICAL / functional] CMS Management: Admin can edit the content for the following CMS pages: About us, Contact us, Privacy policy, and Terms and conditions.
24. [HIGH / functional] Statistics & Reports: Admin can view reports on Products uploaded (filterable by Date: From-To, Month, Year) and Revenue/total sale (filterable by Today, Current week, Date: From-To, Month, Year). Reports can be exported to PDF and Excel formats.
25. [HIGH / functional] System Users Management: Admin can create/edit/delete/activate/inactivate sub-users for various sectional operations.
26. [HIGH / functional] Roles Management: Admin can add/edit/delete/activate/inactivate sub-admin users with role-based access.
27. [HIGH / functional] Complaints/Feedbacks: Admin can view queries/complaints/feedbacks received from buyers (via FR-013). The admin will also receive an email notification for each submission.
28. [MEDIUM / functional] Email Management: Admin can add/edit/delete content for emails to be sent to buyers regarding new product launch, offers, and promotions.
29. [MEDIUM / non-functional] Scalability: The website repository shall accommodate up to 100 concurrent users.
30. [MEDIUM / non-functional] Speed/Performance: Web pages should load in less than 3 seconds under good internet speed.
31. [MEDIUM / non-functional] Reliability/Availability: Web pages must not display "page not found" errors for non-existent pages.
32. [MEDIUM / non-functional] Security: SSL security and encryption are mandatory for online payments.
33. [HIGH / non-functional] Page Load Speed shall not exceed 3 seconds.
34. [HIGH / non-functional] API Response Time shall not exceed 500 milliseconds.
35. [HIGH / non-functional] Search Latency shall not exceed 1 second.
36. [HIGH / non-functional] Must accommodate up to 100 users concurrently.
37. [HIGH / non-functional] Must support a minimum of 150 orders per hour.
38. [HIGH / non-functional] Must support a minimum of 10,000 product SKUs.
39. [HIGH / non-functional] SSL security and encryption (Minimum TLS 1.2).
40. [HIGH / non-functional] Passwords must be stored using a one-way hashing algorithm (e.g., bcrypt or Argon2) with salt.
41. [HIGH / non-functional] Must enforce Role-Based Access Control (RBAC) for all Admin and Sub-user functions.
42. [HIGH / non-functional] System must enforce input validation against SQL Injection and Cross-Site Scripting (XSS) on all user and admin inputs.
43. [HIGH / non-functional] 99.9% uptime during core business hours (9 AM - 5 PM EST).
44. [HIGH / non-functional] Web pages should not get broken and must display an appropriate "Page Not Found" error.
45. [HIGH / non-functional] Daily full backup; retention for 30 days.
46. [HIGH / non-functional] Must log all create/edit/delete operations performed by Admin and Sub-users.
47. [HIGH / non-functional] All configurable values (e.g., Tax rates, Shipping carrier details, Email content) must be managed via the Admin Panel.
48. [HIGH / non-functional] Codebase must adhere to [Specific Language] coding standards (e.g., PEP8 for Python) and pass peer review.
49. [HIGH / non-functional] US country only. System must validate shipping addresses for US residency.
50. [HIGH / non-functional] All product prices will be in USD.
51. [HIGH / non-functional] CMS pages for Privacy Policy and Terms and Conditions must be accessible and editable by the Admin.

## Features

1. **Account Management (Login/Registration)**: Allows users to log in, register, and manage their account details.
2. **Product Search**: Enables buyers/guests to search for products by keyword, category, and filters.
3. **Product Listing**: Displays product information such as title, image, price, and ratings.
4. **Product Details**: Shows detailed information about a product, including images, description, price, and variations.
5. **Wishlist**: Allows buyers to add products to their wishlist.
6. **Shopping Cart**: Enables users to add/remove items and update quantities in their shopping cart.
7. **Checkout & Payment**: Facilitates the checkout process, including billing/shipping address input and online payment.
8. **Order History & Tracking**: Allows buyers to view their past orders and track the status of current orders.
9. **Ratings & Reviews**: Enables users to post ratings and reviews for products.
10. **Social Media Sharing**: Allows buyers/guests to share products on social media.
11. **Contact Support**: Enables buyers/guests to contact support via email.
12. **Admin Login**: Allows admin/sub-users to log in to the admin panel.
13. **Dashboard**: Displays key metrics on the admin dashboard.
14. **Products Management**: Allows admin to manage products in the catalog.
15. **Product Categories Management**: Allows admin to manage product categories and sub-categories.
16. **Orders Management**: Allows admin to view and manage orders.
17. **Shipping Management**: Allows admin to manage shipping details.
18. **Buyers Management**: Allows admin to manage buyer accounts.
19. **Ratings & Review Management**: Allows admin to approve/reject ratings and reviews.
20. **Payment Management**: Allows admin to manage payment details.
21. **CMS Management**: Allows admin to edit CMS pages.
22. **Statistics & Reports**: Allows admin to view reports on products and revenue.
23. **System Users Management**: Allows admin to manage sub-users.
24. **Roles Management**: Allows admin to manage sub-admin roles.
25. **Complaints/Feedbacks**: Allows admin to view complaints/feedbacks from buyers.
26. **Email Management**: Allows admin to manage email content.
27. **Buyer Login**: Allows buyers to login using email/password or social media accounts.
28. **Buyer Registration**: Allows buyers to register on the website.
29. **Product Search**: Enables buyers to search for products using keywords, categories, filters, and sorting.
30. **Product Listing**: Displays a list of products with details like title, image, price, ratings, and reviews.
31. **Product Details**: Shows detailed information about a product, including images, description, price, sizes, colors, and shipping availability.
32. **Wishlist**: Allows buyers to save products to a wishlist.
33. **Shopping Cart**: Enables buyers to add, remove, and update items in their shopping cart.
34. **Checkout & Payment**: Facilitates the checkout and payment process, including billing and shipping address entry and payment method selection.
35. **Social Media Sharing**: Allows users to share products on social media platforms.
36. **My Account**: Provides buyers with a section to manage their profile details, orders, wishlist, and reviews.
37. **Ratings & Reviews**: Allows buyers to rate and review products they have ordered.
38. **Order History**: Displays a list of past orders with details and tracking information.
39. **Contact Support**: Enables buyers to contact the support team with queries or complaints.
40. **Admin Login**: Allows the admin to login to the admin panel.
41. **Dashboard**: Displays key information like total buyers, products, and revenue.
42. **Buyers Management**: Allows the admin to manage buyer accounts.
43. **Orders Management**: Allows the admin to manage orders and update their status.
44. **Product Categories Management**: Allows the admin to manage product categories and sub-categories.
45. **Products Management**: Allows the admin to manage product information.
46. **Ratings & Review Management**: Allows the admin to approve/reject ratings and reviews.
47. **Statistics & Reports**: Provides various reports on products and revenue.
48. **System Users Management**: Allows the admin to manage sub-users.
49. **Roles Management**: Allows the admin to manage roles and permissions for sub-users.
50. **CMS Management**: Allows the admin to edit content for CMS pages like About Us and Contact Us.
51. **Email Management**: Allows the admin to manage email content for promotions and notifications.
52. **Complaints/Feedbacks**: Allows the admin to view and respond to buyer complaints and feedback.
53. **Search Functionality**: Implement a server-side full-text search engine to handle keyword and category search efficiently.
54. **Product Variations**: The Product Details Page must dynamically handle color and size variations and update the display based on availability.
55. **Shipping Check**: An API call must be made to a shipping service or internal table based on the entered PIN code to check availability.
56. **Login/Registration**: Implement OAuth 2.0 or OpenID Connect flows for third-party logins. Passwords must be hashed and salted.
57. **Mandatory Verification**: Implement an asynchronous job or service to send the email verification link upon registration.
58. **Secure Transactions**: All checkout and payment pages must enforce HTTPS and interact with the Stripe API securely using tokens.
59. **Role-Based Access Control (RBAC)**: Implement a granular RBAC system allowing the main Admin to create sub-users and assign them specific roles/permissions.
60. **Catalog Management**: Utilize a Content Management System (CMS) interface within the Admin Panel to manage product attributes.
61. **Inventory Integration**: The system will use the Product Code (SKU) as the key for integrating with any future inventory management tools.
62. **Order Status Workflow**: Implement a state machine for order status transitions with automated email notifications to the buyer upon each change.
63. **Data Aggregation**: Implement a data layer optimized for reporting to quickly generate reports for Products Uploaded and Revenue/Total Sale.
64. **Export Functionality**: Use a library to generate and export reports into standard PDF and Excel formats.
65. **Registration**: User registration functionality.
66. **Login (Email/Social)**: User login functionality using email or social media accounts.
67. **Product Search/Listing**: Functionality to search and list products.
68. **Product Details/Variations**: Displaying product details and variations.
69. **Shopping Cart**: Functionality to add and manage items in a shopping cart.
70. **Wishlist**: Functionality to save products to a wishlist.
71. **Checkout**: Checkout process for ordering products.
72. **Online Payment (Stripe)**: Online payment processing using Stripe.
73. **Order Tracking**: Functionality to track orders.
74. **Ratings & Reviews**: Functionality to rate and review products.
75. **My Account/Address Book**: User account management and address book.
76. **Admin Login**: Admin login functionality.
77. **Dashboard**: Admin dashboard with key metrics.
78. **Product/Category Management**: Functionality to manage products and categories.
79. **Orders Management**: Functionality to manage orders.
80. **Customer Management**: Functionality to manage customers.
81. **Shipping/Payment Management**: Functionality to manage shipping and payment options.
82. **CMS**: Content Management System for managing website content.
83. **Roles/Permissions**: Functionality to manage user roles and permissions.
84. **Reporting (Statistics)**: Reporting and statistics functionality.

## Technical Context

**Technologies:** SSL, bcrypt

**Architecture (Functional Specification Document.pdf):** Frontend website for buyers and a web-based backend/admin panel for the business owner.

**Architecture (Technical Specification Document.pdf):** Three-Tier Architecture (Presentation, Application/Business Logic, and Data)
**Tech Stack:** HTML5, CSS3, JavaScript, React, Vue.js, Python, Django, Node.js, Express, PHP, Laravel, PostgreSQL, MySQL, Stripe, Elasticsearch, bcrypt, Pandas

**Architecture (Test Plan.pdf):** Phased approach, utilizing different types of testing to ensure quality at various stages of development.

### Planning Guidelines
- Since all documents are pre-loaded in the context, you can directly use LLM to analyze them without FileReader.
- Use LLM to:
  - Identify epics and high-level modules.
  - Break epics into user stories and acceptance criteria.
  - Extract non-functional requirements (performance, scalability, security, etc.).
  - Identify dependencies and constraints.
  - Propose milestones and phases.
  - Highlight risks and assumptions.
- Use Google only when clarifications or standards are needed.

## ðŸ¤– LLM Interaction #2: Tool Execution - LLM

### Context

- **Evidence ID:** #E1
- **Tool:** LLM
- **Step:** 1

### Complete Prompt Sent to LLM

```
Extract project goals and objectives from the pre-loaded documents, focusing on the business requirements, functional specifications, and use cases. Identify the primary objectives for both the buyer-facing website and the admin panel.
```

### LLM Response

```
Okay, I need the pre-loaded documents to do this.  Please provide the text of the documents.  Once you provide the text, I will:

1.  **Analyze the documents** for sections related to:
    *   Business Requirements
    *   Functional Specifications
    *   Use Cases

2.  **Extract Goals and Objectives** from these sections, focusing on what the system needs to achieve.  I will look for statements that describe desired outcomes, functionalities, and user interactions.

3.  **Categorize the Objectives** into two primary areas:
    *   **Buyer-Facing Website:**  Objectives related to the customer experience, browsing, purchasing, account management, etc.
    *   **Admin Panel:** Objectives related to managing products, orders, users, content, and other administrative tasks.

4.  **Present the Extracted Information:** I will organize the extracted goals and objectives in a clear and concise manner, likely using bullet points, to distinguish between the buyer-facing website and the admin panel.

**Example (What I will do once you provide the documents):**

Let's say a document contained the following snippets:

*   "Business Requirement:  Customers must be able to easily search for products based on keywords, categories, and price range."
*   "Functional Specification: The website shall display product images, descriptions, and customer reviews."
*   "Use Case:  An administrator needs to be able to add new product categories through the admin panel."

Then, I would extract and present the information like this:

**Buyer-Facing Website:**

*   **Goal:**  Enable customers to easily find desired products.
*   **Objective:**  Implement product search functionality based on keywords, categories, and price range.
*   **Objective:**  Display comprehensive product information, including images, descriptions, and customer reviews.

**Admin Panel:**

*   **Goal:**  Provide administrators with the tools to manage product catalog.
*   **Objective:**  Allow administrators to add and manage product categories.

**Please provide the text of the documents so I can perform the analysis.**
```

## ðŸ¤– LLM Interaction #3: Tool Execution - LLM

### Context

- **Evidence ID:** #E2
- **Tool:** LLM
- **Step:** 2

### Complete Prompt Sent to LLM

```
Define measurable success metrics (KPIs) based on the extracted project goals and objectives. Include metrics for user engagement (e.g., conversion rate, average order value), system performance (e.g., page load time, API response time), and operational efficiency (e.g., order processing time, customer support response time). Also incorporate the non-functional requirements related to scalability and security.
```

### LLM Response

```
Okay, let's define measurable success metrics (KPIs) based on typical project goals and objectives, incorporating user engagement, system performance, operational efficiency, scalability, and security.  Since I don't have specific project goals and objectives, I'll use common examples and provide a framework you can adapt.

**Assumed Project Goals & Objectives (Examples):**

*   **Goal 1: Increase Revenue:**
    *   Objective 1: Increase online sales.
    *   Objective 2: Increase average order value.
*   **Goal 2: Improve User Experience:**
    *   Objective 1: Reduce user frustration.
    *   Objective 2: Increase user engagement.
*   **Goal 3: Enhance System Performance:**
    *   Objective 1: Reduce page load times.
    *   Objective 2: Improve system stability.
*   **Goal 4: Streamline Operations:**
    *   Objective 1: Reduce order processing time.
    *   Objective 2: Improve customer support efficiency.
*   **Non-Functional Requirements:**
    *   Scalability:  Handle a 50% increase in traffic within the next year without performance degradation.
    *   Security:  Maintain the confidentiality, integrity, and availability of user data and system resources.

**Measurable Success Metrics (KPIs):**

Here's a breakdown of KPIs, categorized by area:

**I. User Engagement:**

| KPI                        | Description                                                                                                                                                              | Measurement Frequency | Target/Threshold                                                                                                                                                              |
| -------------------------- | ------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------ | --------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Conversion Rate**         | Percentage of website visitors who complete a desired action (e.g., purchase, sign-up, form submission).  Calculated as (Number of Conversions / Number of Visitors) * 100 | Weekly/Monthly        | Increase from X% to Y% within [timeframe].  Maintain above Z%.                                                                                                          |
| **Average Order Value (AOV)** | Average amount spent per order.  Calculated as (Total Revenue / Number of Orders).                                                                                        | Weekly/Monthly        | Increase from $X to $Y within [timeframe].                                                                                                                                 |
| **Bounce Rate**             | Percentage of visitors who leave the website after viewing only one page.                                                                                              | Weekly/Monthly        | Decrease from X% to Y% within [timeframe].  Maintain below Z%.                                                                                                          |
| **Pages per Session**       | Average number of pages a user views during a single session on the website.                                                                                             | Weekly/Monthly        | Increase from X to Y within [timeframe].                                                                                                                                    |
| **Time on Site/Session Duration** | Average amount of time a user spends on the website during a single session.                                                                                                | Weekly/Monthly        | Increase from X minutes to Y minutes within [timeframe].                                                                                                                   |
| **Customer Acquisition Cost (CAC)** | The cost of acquiring a new customer.  (Total Marketing Spend / Number of New Customers).                                                                                 | Monthly/Quarterly     | Reduce from $X to $Y within [timeframe].                                                                                                                                 |
| **Customer Lifetime Value (CLTV)** | A prediction of the net profit attributed to the entire future relationship with a customer.                                                                                 | Monthly/Quarterly     | Increase from $X to $Y within [timeframe].                                                                                                                                 |
| **Net Promoter Score (NPS)** | Measures customer loyalty and willingness to recommend the product/service.                                                                                            | Quarterly             | Increase from X to Y within [timeframe].  Achieve a score above Z.                                                                                                      |
| **User Satisfaction (CSAT)** | Measures customer satisfaction with a specific interaction or feature.                                                                                                 | After Interaction     | Achieve an average score of Y out of Z.                                                                                                                                    |
| **Feature Usage Rate** | Percentage of users actively using a specific feature. | Weekly/Monthly | Increase from X% to Y% within [timeframe]. |

**II. System Performance:**

| KPI                     | Description                                                                                                                                                                        | Measurement Frequency | Target/Threshold                                                                                                                                                                                                       |
| ----------------------- | ---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- | --------------------- | --------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| **Page Load Time**      | Time it takes for a web page to fully load.                                                                                                                                       | Continuously/Daily    | Average page load time should be less than X seconds (e.g., 3 seconds) for Y% of pages. Specific pages (e.g., homepage, product pages) should load in under Z seconds.                                                                                                  |
| **API Response Time**   | Time it takes for an API to respond to a request.                                                                                                                                  | Continuously/Daily    | Average API response time should be less than X milliseconds (e.g., 200ms) for Y% of requests. Critical APIs should respond in under Z milliseconds.                                                                                                |
| **Error Rate**          | Percentage of requests that result in an error (e.g., 500 errors, 404 errors).                                                                                                      | Continuously/Daily    | Error rate should be less than X% (e.g., 0.1%). Identify and address the root cause of errors exceeding this threshold.                                                                                               |
| **Uptime**              | Percentage of time the system is available and operational.                                                                                                                         | Continuously/Daily    | Achieve X% uptime (e.g., 99.99%).                                                                                                                                                                                    |
| **CPU Utilization**       | Percentage of CPU resources being used.                                                                                                                                           | Continuously/Daily    | Maintain average CPU utilization below X% (e.g., 70%). Identify and address spikes in CPU usage.                                                                                                                     |
| **Memory Utilization**    | Percentage of memory resources being used.                                                                                                                                        | Continuously/Daily    | Maintain average memory utilization below X% (e.g., 80%). Identify and address memory leaks.                                                                                                                       |
| **Database Query Time** | Time it takes for database queries to execute.                                                                                                                                      | Continuously/Daily    | Average database query time should be less than X milliseconds (e.g., 50ms). Optimize slow-running queries.                                                                                                                   |
| **Throughput**          | Number of requests or transactions processed per unit of time (e.g., requests per second, transactions per minute).                                                               | Continuously/Daily    | Maintain a throughput of at least X requests per second under normal load. Ensure the system can handle Y requests per second during peak load.                                                                                |
| **Time to first byte (TTFB)** | The time it takes for the browser to receive the first byte of data from the server. | Continuously/Daily |  Keep TTFB under X milliseconds (e.g., 100ms). |

## ðŸ¤– LLM Interaction #4: Tool Execution - LLM

### Context

- **Evidence ID:** #E3
- **Tool:** LLM
- **Step:** 3

### Complete Prompt Sent to LLM

```
Identify key stakeholders and define their roles (Driver, Approver, Contributors, Informed) based on the project documents and the feasibility assessment. Consider roles such as the client (Approver), project manager (Driver), frontend developers, backend developers, QA testers, UI/UX designer, and DevOps engineer (Contributors).
